Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

T dependence: `T^2/(T+c1)` and linear T terms. No exp(-c/T). The `T^2/(T+c1)` term can approximate linear T for large T but is never exactly linear. Also needs epsilon^0.4776 and epsilon^3 which aren't present. Cannot match.
Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 19:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + T*c2*epsilon^c3 + c4*epsilon*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6 + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon^c3`
Has T*c2*epsilon^c3. If c3=3, this gives T*epsilon^3. Also has T*c0*epsilon (set c0=0), T*c1 (set c1=0). Then remaining: T*c2*epsilon^3 + c4*epsilon*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6 + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon^3.
GT needs: epsilon^0.4776*exp(-c/T) + T*epsilon^3 - const*epsilon^3.
The c8*epsilon^3 can provide the -const*epsilon^3 term. But we need epsilon^0.4776*exp(-c/T), and this candidate has c4*epsilon*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6 + c7*epsilon — none of which involve exp(-c/T) or epsilon^0.4776. Cannot match.
Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]
